\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_decoder}{Decoder}} is not a preferred choice for probing. This indicates that the decoder is not a good choice for probing. It could for example be an expensive to spin up hardware decoder, or it could simply not provide a lot of useful information about the stream. A decoder marked with this flag should only be used as last resort choice for probing.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ga3f55f5bcfbb12e06c7cb1195028855e6}\label{group__lavc__core_ga3f55f5bcfbb12e06c7cb1195028855e6}} 
\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY@{AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY}}
\index{AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY@{AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY}{AV\_CODEC\_CAP\_DELAY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+AY~(1 $<$$<$  5)}

Encoder or decoder requires flushing with N\+U\+LL input at the end in order to give the complete and correct output.

N\+O\+TE\+: If this flag is not set, the codec is guaranteed to never be fed with with N\+U\+LL data. The user can still send N\+U\+LL data to the public encode or decode function, but libavcodec will not pass it along to the codec unless this flag is set.

Decoders\+: The decoder has a non-\/zero delay and needs to be fed with avpkt-\/$>$data=N\+U\+LL, avpkt-\/$>$size=0 at the end to get the delayed data until the decoder no longer returns frames.

Encoders\+: The encoder needs to be fed with N\+U\+LL data at the end of encoding until the encoder no longer returns data.

N\+O\+TE\+: For encoders implementing the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_ae6a4bce1a04a3e2e8dea84ffe133f18a}{A\+V\+Codec.\+encode2()}} function, setting this flag also means that the encoder must set the pts and duration for each output packet. If this flag is not set, the pts and duration will be determined by libavcodec from the input frame.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+B\+F\+R\+A\+M\+ES~(1 $<$$<$  8)}

Codec can output multiple frames per \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_packet}{A\+V\+Packet}} Normally demuxers return one frame at a time, demuxers which do not do are connected to a parser to split what they return into proper frames. This flag is reserved to the very rare category of codecs which have a bitstream that cannot be split into frames without timeconsuming operations like full decoding. Demuxers carrying such bitstreams thus may return multiple frames in a packet. This has many disadvantages like prohibiting stream copy in many cases thus it should only be considered as a last resort.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AV\_CODEC\_PROP\_REORDER}{AV\_CODEC\_PROP\_REORDER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+O\+R\+D\+ER~(1 $<$$<$ 3)}

Codec supports frame reordering. That is, the coded order (the order in which the encoded packets are output by the encoders / stored / input to the decoders) may be different from the presentation order of the corresponding frames.

For codecs that do not have this property set, P\+TS and D\+TS should always be equal.

The bitstream filter state.

This struct must be allocated with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga7da65af303e20c9546e15ec266b182c1}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+alloc()}} and freed with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga08d53431e76355f88e27763b1940df4f}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+free()}}.

The fields in the struct will only be changed (by the caller or by the filter) as described in their documentation, and are to be considered immutable otherwise. \mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ga8ef1664899e2596939d922e9c589094c}\label{group__lavc__core_ga8ef1664899e2596939d922e9c589094c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}}}

main external A\+PI structure. New fields can be added to the end with minor version bumps. Removal, reordering and changes to existing fields require a major version bump. You can use A\+V\+Options (av\+\_\+opt$\ast$ / av\+\_\+set/get$\ast$()) to access these fields from user applications. The name string for A\+V\+Options options matches the associated command line parameter name and can be found in libavcodec/options\+\_\+table.\+h The A\+V\+Option/command line parameter names differ in some cases from the C structure field names for historic reasons or brevity. sizeof(\+A\+V\+Codec\+Context) must not be used outside libav$\ast$. \mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ga27561af66de4a75c3da1dc61f8c5cd9a}\label{group__lavc__core_ga27561af66de4a75c3da1dc61f8c5cd9a}}

A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_acf8113e490f9e7b57465e65af9c0c75c}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx}} should have been set to a device of the specified type before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}\label{group__lavc__core_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+S\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format for a decoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to a suitable frames context inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{doc_2examples_2qsvdec_8c_afe1023087c26d2d410c9cd7d491c8660}{get\+\_\+format()}} callback. The frames context must have been created on a device of the specified type.

When selecting this format for an encoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to the context which will be used for the input frames before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa7386da6a6a78eb809d838053e4035ee}\label{group__lavc__core_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa7386da6a6a78eb809d838053e4035ee}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+AL&The codec supports this format by some internal method.

This format can be selected without any additional configuration -\/ no device or frames context is required. \\

Definition at line 239 of file avcodec.\+h.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_gaadca229ad2c20e060a14fec08a5cc7ce}\label{group__lavc__core_gaadca229ad2c20e060a14fec08a5cc7ce}} 
\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!AVCodecID@{AVCodecID}}
\index{AVCodecID@{AVCodecID}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AVCodecID}{AVCodecID}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaadca229ad2c20e060a14fec08a5cc7ce}{A\+V\+Codec\+ID}}}

Identify the syntax and semantics of the bitstream. The principle is roughly\+: Two decoders with the same ID can decode the same streams. Two encoders with the same ID can encode compatible streams. There may be slight deviations from the principle due to implementation details.

If you add a codec ID to this list, add it so that
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item no value of an existing codec ID changes (that would break A\+BI),
\item it is as close as possible to similar codecs
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

After adding new codec I\+Ds, do not forget to add an entry to the codec descriptor list and bump libavcodec minor version. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_ID\_NONE@{AV\_CODEC\_ID\_NONE}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!AV\_CODEC\_ID\_NONE@{AV\_CODEC\_ID\_NONE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ggaadca229ad2c20e060a14fec08a5cc7cea48761c50b102343e2648c3e28a94e7ab}\label{group__lavc__core_ggaadca229ad2c20e060a14fec08a5cc7cea48761c50b102343e2648c3e28a94e7ab}}

\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ga7da65af303e20c9546e15ec266b182c1}\label{group__lavc__core_ga7da65af303e20c9546e15ec266b182c1}} 
\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!av\_bsf\_alloc@{av\_bsf\_alloc}}
\index{av\_bsf\_alloc@{av\_bsf\_alloc}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_bsf\_alloc()}{av\_bsf\_alloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+alloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_bit_stream_filter}{A\+V\+Bit\+Stream\+Filter}} $\ast$}]{filter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{ctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Allocate a context for a given bitstream filter. The caller must fill in the context parameters as described in the documentation and then call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga242529d54013acf87e94273d298a5ff2}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+init()}} before sending any data to the filter.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em filter} & the filter for which to allocate an instance. \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & a pointer into which the pointer to the newly-\/allocated context will be written. It must be freed with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga08d53431e76355f88e27763b1940df4f}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+free()}} after the filtering is done.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, a negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR code on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_list}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+List}}$\ast$ av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+alloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Allocate empty list of bitstream filters. The list must be later freed by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga0e144e330612e37a23acf056db4ac220}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+free()}} or finalized by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaa4f71b6265b76b23abd418b62ffaff2d}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+finalize()}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_bsf\_list\_finalize()}{av\_bsf\_list\_finalize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+finalize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_list}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+List}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{lst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{bsf }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Finalize list of bitstream filters.

This function will transform \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_list}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+List}} to single \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}}, so the whole chain of bitstream filters can be treated as single filter freshly allocated by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga7da65af303e20c9546e15ec266b182c1}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+alloc()}}. If the call is successful, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_list}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+List}} structure is freed and lst will be set to N\+U\+LL. In case of failure, caller is responsible for freeing the structure by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga0e144e330612e37a23acf056db4ac220}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+free()}}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em lst} & Filter list structure to be transformed \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em bsf} & Pointer to be set to newly created \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} structure representing the chain of bitstream filters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
$>$=0 on success, negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR in case of failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str@{av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str}}
\index{av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str@{av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str()}{av\_bsf\_list\_parse\_str()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+list\+\_\+parse\+\_\+str (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{bsf }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Parse string describing list of bitstream filters and create single \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} describing the whole chain of bitstream filters. Resulting \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} can be treated as any other \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} freshly allocated by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga7da65af303e20c9546e15ec266b182c1}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+alloc()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em str} & String describing chain of bitstream filters in format {\ttfamily bsf1\mbox{[}=opt1=val1\+:opt2=val2\mbox{]}\mbox{[},bsf2\mbox{]}} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em bsf} & Pointer to be set to newly created \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} structure representing the chain of bitstream filters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
$>$=0 on success, negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR in case of failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!av\_bsf\_receive\_packet@{av\_bsf\_receive\_packet}}
\index{av\_bsf\_receive\_packet@{av\_bsf\_receive\_packet}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_bsf\_receive\_packet()}{av\_bsf\_receive\_packet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+receive\+\_\+packet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_packet}{A\+V\+Packet}} $\ast$}]{pkt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Retrieve a filtered packet.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pkt} & this struct will be filled with the contents of the filtered packet. It is owned by the caller and must be freed using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__packet_ga63d5a489b419bd5d45cfd09091cbcbc2}{av\+\_\+packet\+\_\+unref()}} when it is no longer needed. This parameter should be \char`\"{}clean\char`\"{} (i.\+e. freshly allocated with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__packet_gaaf85aa950695631e0217a16062289b66}{av\+\_\+packet\+\_\+alloc()}} or unreffed with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__packet_ga63d5a489b419bd5d45cfd09091cbcbc2}{av\+\_\+packet\+\_\+unref()}}) when this function is called. If this function returns successfully, the contents of pkt will be completely overwritten by the returned data. On failure, pkt is not touched.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success. \mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_adf2fb515710d47541f7150ecd2950e76}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+A\+G\+A\+I\+N)}} if more packets need to be sent to the filter (using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaada9ea8f08d3dcf23c14564dbc88992c}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+send\+\_\+packet()}}) to get more output. A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+OF if there will be no further output from the filter. Another negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR value if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
one input packet may result in several output packets, so after sending a packet with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaada9ea8f08d3dcf23c14564dbc88992c}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+send\+\_\+packet()}}, this function needs to be called repeatedly until it stops returning 0. It is also possible for a filter to output fewer packets than were sent to it, so this function may return \mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_adf2fb515710d47541f7150ecd2950e76}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+A\+G\+A\+I\+N)}} immediately after a successful \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaada9ea8f08d3dcf23c14564dbc88992c}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+send\+\_\+packet()}} call. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{av\_bsf\_send\_packet@{av\_bsf\_send\_packet}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_bsf\_send\_packet()}{av\_bsf\_send\_packet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+send\+\_\+packet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_b_s_f_context}{A\+V\+B\+S\+F\+Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_packet}{A\+V\+Packet}} $\ast$}]{pkt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Submit a packet for filtering.

After sending each packet, the filter must be completely drained by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga7fffb6c87b91250956e7a2367af56b38}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+receive\+\_\+packet()}} repeatedly until it returns \mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_adf2fb515710d47541f7150ecd2950e76}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+A\+G\+A\+I\+N)}} or A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+OF.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pkt} & the packet to filter. The bitstream filter will take ownership of the packet and reset the contents of pkt. pkt is not touched if an error occurs. If pkt is empty (i.\+e. N\+U\+LL, or pkt-\/$>$data is N\+U\+LL and pkt-\/$>$side\+\_\+data\+\_\+elems zero), it signals the end of the stream (i.\+e. no more non-\/empty packets will be sent; sending more empty packets does nothing) and will cause the filter to output any packets it may have buffered internally.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success. \mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_adf2fb515710d47541f7150ecd2950e76}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+A\+G\+A\+I\+N)}} if packets need to be retrieved from the filter (using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga7fffb6c87b91250956e7a2367af56b38}{av\+\_\+bsf\+\_\+receive\+\_\+packet()}}) before new input can be consumed. Another negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR value if an error occurs. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!avcodec\_alloc\_context3@{avcodec\_alloc\_context3}}
\index{avcodec\_alloc\_context3@{avcodec\_alloc\_context3}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_alloc\_context3()}{avcodec\_alloc\_context3()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}}$\ast$ avcodec\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+context3 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec}{A\+V\+Codec}} $\ast$}]{codec }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Allocate an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} and set its fields to default values. The resulting struct should be freed with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaf869d0829ed607cec3a4a02a1c7026b3}{avcodec\+\_\+free\+\_\+context()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em codec} & if non-\/\+N\+U\+LL, allocate private data and initialize defaults for the given codec. It is illegal to then call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}} with a different codec. If N\+U\+LL, then the codec-\/specific defaults won\textquotesingle{}t be initialized, which may result in suboptimal default settings (this is important mainly for encoders, e.\+g. libx264).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} filled with default values or N\+U\+LL on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_gaf4daa92361efb3523ef5afeb0b54077f}\label{group__lavc__core_gaf4daa92361efb3523ef5afeb0b54077f}} 
\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!avcodec\_close@{avcodec\_close}}
\index{avcodec\_close@{avcodec\_close}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_close()}{avcodec\_close()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} avcodec\+\_\+close (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{avctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Close a given \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} and free all the data associated with it (but not the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} itself).

Calling this function on an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} that hasn\textquotesingle{}t been opened will free the codec-\/specific data allocated in \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gae80afec6f26df6607eaacf39b561c315}{avcodec\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+context3()}} with a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL codec. Subsequent calls will do nothing.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Do not use this function. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaf869d0829ed607cec3a4a02a1c7026b3}{avcodec\+\_\+free\+\_\+context()}} to destroy a codec context (either open or closed). Opening and closing a codec context multiple times is not supported anymore -- use multiple codec contexts instead. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{avcodec\_copy\_context@{avcodec\_copy\_context}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_copy\_context()}{avcodec\_copy\_context()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{libswscale_2utils_8c_aa6d076561d3a9eea4729ee632652de02}{attribute\+\_\+deprecated}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} avcodec\+\_\+copy\+\_\+context (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{dest,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{src }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copy the settings of the source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} into the destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}}. The resulting destination codec context will be unopened, i.\+e. you are required to call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}} before you can use this \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} to decode/encode video/audio data.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dest} & target codec context, should be initialized with avcodec\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+context3(\+N\+U\+L\+L), but otherwise uninitialized \\
\hline
{\em src} & source codec context \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_adf2fb515710d47541f7150ecd2950e76}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R()}} on error (e.\+g. memory allocation error), 0 on success
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000003}{Deprecated}}]The semantics of this function are ill-\/defined and it should not be used. If you need to transfer the stream parameters from one codec context to another, use an intermediate \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_parameters}{A\+V\+Codec\+Parameters}} instance and the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga0c7058f764778615e7978a1821ab3cfe}{avcodec\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+from\+\_\+context()}} / \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gac7b282f51540ca7a99416a3ba6ee0d16}{avcodec\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+to\+\_\+context()}} functions. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_get\_hw\_config()}{avcodec\_get\_hw\_config()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_h_w_config}{A\+V\+Codec\+H\+W\+Config}}$\ast$ avcodec\+\_\+get\+\_\+hw\+\_\+config (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec}{A\+V\+Codec}} $\ast$}]{codec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Retrieve supported hardware configurations for a codec.

Values of index from zero to some maximum return the indexed configuration descriptor; all other values return N\+U\+LL. If the codec does not support any hardware configurations then it will always return N\+U\+LL.

Definition at line 1484 of file utils.\+c.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}\label{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}} 
\index{Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}!avcodec\_open2@{avcodec\_open2}}
\index{avcodec\_open2@{avcodec\_open2}!Core functions/structures.@{Core functions/structures.}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_open2()}{avcodec\_open2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} avcodec\+\_\+open2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{avctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec}{A\+V\+Codec}} $\ast$}]{codec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_dictionary}{A\+V\+Dictionary}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initialize the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} to use the given \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec}{A\+V\+Codec}}. Prior to using this function the context has to be allocated with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gae80afec6f26df6607eaacf39b561c315}{avcodec\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+context3()}}.

The functions \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga776f2359007e8457799503068419e791}{avcodec\+\_\+find\+\_\+decoder\+\_\+by\+\_\+name()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gaa614ffc38511c104bdff4a3afa086d37}{avcodec\+\_\+find\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+by\+\_\+name()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga19a0ca553277f019dd5b0fec6e1f9dca}{avcodec\+\_\+find\+\_\+decoder()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga9f820c481615c3a02d0407bac0bdbf25}{avcodec\+\_\+find\+\_\+encoder()}} provide an easy way for retrieving a codec.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function is not thread safe!
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Always call this function before using decoding routines (such as \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__decoding_ga11e6542c4e66d3028668788a1a74217c}{avcodec\+\_\+receive\+\_\+frame()}}).
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em avctx} & The context to initialize. \\
\hline
{\em codec} & The codec to open this context for. If a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL codec has been previously passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_gae80afec6f26df6607eaacf39b561c315}{avcodec\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+context3()}} or for this context, then this parameter M\+U\+ST be either N\+U\+LL or equal to the previously passed codec. \\
\hline
{\em options} & A dictionary filled with \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} and codec-\/private options. On return this object will be filled with options that were not found.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

zero on success, a negative value on error

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} avcodec\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+from\+\_\+context (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_parameters}{A\+V\+Codec\+Parameters}} $\ast$}]{par,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{codec }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_parameters\_to\_context()}{avcodec\_parameters\_to\_context()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} avcodec\+\_\+parameters\+\_\+to\+\_\+context (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{codec,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_parameters}{A\+V\+Codec\+Parameters}} $\ast$}]{par }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Fill the codec context based on the values from the supplied codec parameters. Any allocated fields in codec that have a corresponding field in par are freed and replaced with duplicates of the corresponding field in par. Fields in codec that do not have a counterpart in par are not touched.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
$>$= 0 on success, a negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR code on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{avcodec\_register\_all()}{avcodec\_register\_all()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{libswscale_2utils_8c_aa6d076561d3a9eea4729ee632652de02}{attribute\+\_\+deprecated}} \mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} avcodec\+\_\+register\+\_\+all (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Register all the codecs, parsers and bitstream filters which were enabled at configuration time. If you do not call this function you can select exactly which formats you want to support, by using the individual registration functions.
